\begin{register}{H}{H264\_DMA\_OUT\_CONF0\_CH0\_REG}{0x0000}\label{regdesc:H264DMAOUTCONF0CH0REG}
\regfield{(reserved)}{5}{27}{00000}%
\regfield{H264\_DMA\_OUT\_ARB\_WEIGHT\_OPT\_DIS\_CH0}{1}{26}{{0}}%
\regfield{H264\_DMA\_OUT\_CMD\_DISABLE\_CH0}{1}{25}{{0}}%
\regfield{H264\_DMA\_OUT\_RST\_CH0}{1}{24}{{0}}%
\regfield{(reserved)}{7}{17}{0000000}%
\regfield{H264\_DMA\_OUT\_REORDER\_EN\_CH0}{1}{16}{{0}}%
\regfield{(reserved)}{3}{13}{000}%
\regfield{H264\_DMA\_OUT\_PAGE\_BOUND\_EN\_CH0}{1}{12}{{0}}%
\regfield{(reserved)}{3}{9}{000}%
\regfield{H264\_DMA\_OUT\_MEM\_BURST\_LENGTH\_CH0}{3}{6}{{0x0}}%
\regfield{(reserved)}{1}{5}{0}%
\regfield{H264\_DMA\_OUT\_CHECK\_OWNER\_CH0}{1}{4}{{0}}%
\regfield{H264\_DMA\_OUT\_ECC\_AES\_EN\_CH0}{1}{3}{{0}}%
\regfield{H264\_DMA\_OUTDSCR\_BURST\_EN\_CH0}{1}{2}{{0}}%
\regfield{H264\_DMA\_OUT\_EOF\_MODE\_CH0}{1}{1}{{1}}%
\regfield{H264\_DMA\_OUT\_AUTO\_WRBACK\_CH0}{1}{0}{{0}}%
\reglabel{Reset}\regnewline%
\begin{regdesc}\begin{reglist}
\label{fielddesc:H264DMAOUTAUTOWRBACKCH0}\item [H264\_DMA\_OUT\_AUTO\_WRBACK\_CH0] Configures whether to enable automatic outlink-writeback when all the data pointed by outlink descriptor has been received. \\0: Disable \\1: Enable\\(R/W)
\label{fielddesc:H264DMAOUTEOFMODECH0}\item [H264\_DMA\_OUT\_EOF\_MODE\_CH0] Configures EOF flag generation mode for TX channel 0.\\0: EOF flag is generated when last data has been pushed into FIFO in DMA \\1: EOF flag is generated when last data has been popped from FIFO in DMA \\(R/W)
\label{fielddesc:H264DMAOUTDSCRBURSTENCH0}\item [H264\_DMA\_OUTDSCR\_BURST\_EN\_CH0] Configures whether to enable INCR burst transfer for TX channel 0 to read descriptors.\\
0: Disable\\
1: Enable\\(R/W)
\label{fielddesc:H264DMAOUTECCAESENCH0}\item [H264\_DMA\_OUT\_ECC\_AES\_EN\_CH0] Configures whether DMA can access external memory space for ECC and AES via TX channel 0.
\\0: Disable access
\\1: Enable access to the ECC/AES area. In this case, the start address of the memory region should be 16-byte aligned. The product of the width and the bytes per pixel must also be 16-byte aligned.\\ (R/W)
\label{fielddesc:H264DMAOUTCHECKOWNERCH0}\item [H264\_DMA\_OUT\_CHECK\_OWNER\_CH0] Configures whether to enable owner bit check for TX channel 0.\\
0: Disable\\
1: Enable \\(R/W)

\item [Continued on the next page...]
\end{reglist}\end{regdesc}
\end{register}


\addtocounter{Regfloat}{-1}
\begin{register}{H}{H264\_DMA\_OUT\_CONF0\_CH0\_REG}{0x0000}
\begin{regdesc}\begin{reglist}
\item [Continued from the previous page...]

\label{fielddesc:H264DMAOUTMEMBURSTLENGTHCH0}\item [H264\_DMA\_OUT\_MEM\_BURST\_LENGTH\_CH0] Configures the burst length for TX channel 0.\\
0: 8 bytes\\
1: 16 bytes\\
2: 32 bytes\\
3: 64 bytes\\
4: 128 bytes\\
5 \verb+~+ 7: Invalid \\(R/W)
\label{fielddesc:H264DMAOUTPAGEBOUNDENCH0}\item [H264\_DMA\_OUT\_PAGE\_BOUND\_EN\_CH0] Configures whether to make sure AXI read data doesn't cross the address boundary which define by mem\_burst\_length.
\\0: AXI read data can cross the address boundary
\\1: AXI read data doesn't cross the address boundary\\(R/W)\label{fielddesc:H264DMAOUTREORDERENCH0}\item [H264\_DMA\_OUT\_REORDER\_EN\_CH0] Configures whether to enable TX channel 0 macro block reorder.
\\0: Disable
\\1: Enable \\(R/W)
\label{fielddesc:H264DMAOUTRSTCH0}\item [H264\_DMA\_OUT\_RST\_CH0] Write 1 then write 0 to reset TX channel 0. (R/W)
\label{fielddesc:H264DMAOUTCMDDISABLECH0}\item [H264\_DMA\_OUT\_CMD\_DISABLE\_CH0] Configures whether to disable command on TX channel 0.\\
0: Disable\\
1: Enable\\(R/W)
\label{fielddesc:H264DMAOUTARBWEIGHTOPTDISCH0}\item [H264\_DMA\_OUT\_ARB\_WEIGHT\_OPT\_DIS\_CH0] Configures whether to disable weight arbitration for TX channel 0.\\
0: Enable\\
1: Disable \\(R/W)
\end{reglist}\end{regdesc}
\end{register}

\begin{register}{H}{H264\_DMA\_OUT\_PUSH\_CH0\_REG}{0x0018}\label{regdesc:H264DMAOUTPUSHCH0REG}
\regfield{(reserved)}{21}{11}{000000000000000000000}%
\regfield{H264\_DMA\_OUTFIFO\_PUSH\_CH0}{1}{10}{{0}}%
\regfield{H264\_DMA\_OUTFIFO\_WDATA\_CH0}{10}{0}{{0x0}}%
\reglabel{Reset}\regnewline%
\begin{regdesc}\begin{reglist}
\label{fielddesc:H264DMAOUTFIFOWDATACH0}\item [H264\_DMA\_OUTFIFO\_WDATA\_CH0] Represents the data that needs to be pushed into DMA TX FIFO. (R/W)
\label{fielddesc:H264DMAOUTFIFOPUSHCH0}\item [H264\_DMA\_OUTFIFO\_PUSH\_CH0] Configures whether to push data into DMA TX FIFO.\\
0: No effect\\
1: Push \\(R/W/SC)
\end{reglist}\end{regdesc}
\end{register}


\begin{register}{H}{H264\_DMA\_OUT\_LINK\_CONF\_CH0\_REG}{0x001C}\label{regdesc:H264DMAOUTLINKCONFCH0REG}
\regfield{(reserved)}{8}{24}{00000000}%
\regfield{H264\_DMA\_OUTLINK\_PARK\_CH0}{1}{23}{{1}}%
\regfield{H264\_DMA\_OUTLINK\_RESTART\_CH0}{1}{22}{{0}}%
\regfield{H264\_DMA\_OUTLINK\_START\_CH0}{1}{21}{{0}}%
\regfield{H264\_DMA\_OUTLINK\_STOP\_CH0}{1}{20}{{0}}%
\regfield{(reserved)}{20}{0}{00000000000000000000}%
\reglabel{Reset}\regnewline%
\begin{regdesc}\begin{reglist}
\label{fielddesc:H264DMAOUTLINKSTOPCH0}\item [H264\_DMA\_OUTLINK\_STOP\_CH0] Configures whether to stop processing the outlink descriptors.\\
0: No effect\\
1: Stop \\ (R/W/SC)
\label{fielddesc:H264DMAOUTLINKSTARTCH0}\item [H264\_DMA\_OUTLINK\_START\_CH0] Configures whether to start processing the outlink descriptors.\\
0: No effect\\
1: Start \\(R/W/SC)
\label{fielddesc:H264DMAOUTLINKRESTARTCH0}\item [H264\_DMA\_OUTLINK\_RESTART\_CH0] Configures whether to restart a new outlink from the last address.\\
0: No effect\\
1: Restart\\(R/W/SC)
\label{fielddesc:H264DMAOUTLINKPARKCH0}\item [H264\_DMA\_OUTLINK\_PARK\_CH0] Represents the status of the transmit descriptor's FSM.
\\0: The outlink descriptor's FSM is working
\\1: The outlink descriptor's FSM is in idle state \\ (RO)
\end{reglist}\end{regdesc}
\end{register}

\begin{register}{H}{H264\_DMA\_OUT\_RO\_PD\_CONF\_CH0\_REG}{0x0044}\label{regdesc:H264DMAOUTROPDCONFCH0REG}
\regfield{(reserved)}{25}{7}{0000000000000000000000000}%
\regfield{H264\_DMA\_OUT\_RO\_RAM\_CLK\_FO\_CH0}{1}{6}{{0}}%
\regfield{H264\_DMA\_OUT\_RO\_RAM\_FORCE\_PU\_CH0}{1}{5}{{1}}%
\regfield{H264\_DMA\_OUT\_RO\_RAM\_FORCE\_PD\_CH0}{1}{4}{{0}}%
\regfield{(reserved)}{4}{0}{0000}%
\reglabel{Reset}\regnewline%
\begin{regdesc}\begin{reglist}
\label{fielddesc:H264DMAOUTRORAMFORCEPDCH0}\item [H264\_DMA\_OUT\_RO\_RAM\_FORCE\_PD\_CH0] Configures whether to force power down for DMA reorder RAM.
\\0: Not force power down
\\1: Force power down\\(R/W)
\label{fielddesc:H264DMAOUTRORAMFORCEPUCH0}\item [H264\_DMA\_OUT\_RO\_RAM\_FORCE\_PU\_CH0] Configures whether to force power up for DMA reorder RAM.
\\0: Not force power up
\\1: Force power up\\(R/W)
\label{fielddesc:H264DMAOUTRORAMCLKFOCH0}\item [H264\_DMA\_OUT\_RO\_RAM\_CLK\_FO\_CH0] Configures whether to force enable clock gating for DMA TX reorder RAM.
\\0: A clock gating will be used when accessing the RAM in DMA
\\1: Force to open the clock and bypass the clock gating when accessing the RAM in DMA\\(R/W)
\end{reglist}\end{regdesc}
\end{register}

\begin{register}{H}{H264\_DMA\_OUT\_CONF0\_CH1\_REG}{0x0100}\label{regdesc:H264DMAOUTCONF0CH1REG}
\regfield{(reserved)}{5}{27}{00000}%
\regfield{H264\_DMA\_OUT\_ARB\_WEIGHT\_OPT\_DIS\_CH1}{1}{26}{{0}}%
\regfield{H264\_DMA\_OUT\_CMD\_DISABLE\_CH1}{1}{25}{{0}}%
\regfield{H264\_DMA\_OUT\_RST\_CH1}{1}{24}{{0}}%
\regfield{(reserved)}{11}{13}{00000000000}%
\regfield{H264\_DMA\_OUT\_PAGE\_BOUND\_EN\_CH1}{1}{12}{{0}}%
\regfield{(reserved)}{3}{9}{000}%
\regfield{H264\_DMA\_OUT\_MEM\_BURST\_LENGTH\_CH1}{3}{6}{{0x0}}%
\regfield{(reserved)}{1}{5}{0}%
\regfield{H264\_DMA\_OUT\_CHECK\_OWNER\_CH1}{1}{4}{{0}}%
\regfield{H264\_DMA\_OUT\_ECC\_AES\_EN\_CH1}{1}{3}{{0}}%
\regfield{H264\_DMA\_OUTDSCR\_BURST\_EN\_CH1}{1}{2}{{0}}%
\regfield{H264\_DMA\_OUT\_EOF\_MODE\_CH1}{1}{1}{{1}}%
\regfield{H264\_DMA\_OUT\_AUTO\_WRBACK\_CH1}{1}{0}{{0}}%
\reglabel{Reset}\regnewline%
\begin{regdesc}\begin{reglist}
\label{fielddesc:H264DMAOUTAUTOWRBACKCH1}\item [H264\_DMA\_OUT\_AUTO\_WRBACK\_CH1] Configures whether to enable automatic outlink-writeback when all the data pointed by outlink descriptor has been received.
\\0: Disable
\\1: Enable\\(R/W)
\label{fielddesc:H264DMAOUTEOFMODECH1}\item [H264\_DMA\_OUT\_EOF\_MODE\_CH1] Configures EOF flag generation mode for TX channel 1.
\\0: EOF flag is generated when last data has been pushed into FIFO in DMA
\\1: EOF flag is generated when last data has been popped from FIFO in DMA \\(R/W)
\label{fielddesc:H264DMAOUTDSCRBURSTENCH1}\item [H264\_DMA\_OUTDSCR\_BURST\_EN\_CH1] Configures whether to enable INCR burst transfer for TX channel 1 to read descriptors.\\
0: Disable\\
1: Enable\\(R/W)
\label{fielddesc:H264DMAOUTECCAESENCH1}\item [H264\_DMA\_OUT\_ECC\_AES\_EN\_CH1] Configures whether DMA can access external memory space for ECC and AES via TX channel 1.
\\0: Not access
\\1: Access ECC/AES area. In this case, the start address of the memory region should be 16-byte aligned. The product of the width and the bytes per pixel must also be 16-byte aligned.\\(R/W)
\label{fielddesc:H264DMAOUTCHECKOWNERCH1}\item [H264\_DMA\_OUT\_CHECK\_OWNER\_CH1] Configures whether to enable owner bit check for TX channel 1.\\
0: Disable\\
1: Enable\\ (R/W)

0: No effect\\
1: Stop\\ (R/W/SC)
\label{fielddesc:H264DMAOUTLINKSTARTCH2}\item [H264\_DMA\_OUTLINK\_START\_CH2] Configures whether to start processing outlink descriptors.\\
0: No effect\\
1: Start \\(R/W/SC)

0: No effect\\
1: Restart\\(R/W/SC)

\\1: The outlink descriptor's FSM is in idle state \\(RO)

\begin{register}{H}{H264\_DMA\_OUT\_CONF0\_CH3\_REG}{0x0300}\label{regdesc:H264DMAOUTCONF0CH3REG}
\regfield{(reserved)}{5}{27}{00000}%
\regfield{H264\_DMA\_OUT\_ARB\_WEIGHT\_OPT\_DIS\_CH3}{1}{26}{{0}}%
\regfield{(reserved)}{13}{13}{0000000000000}%
\regfield{H264\_DMA\_OUT\_PAGE\_BOUND\_EN\_CH3}{1}{12}{{0}}%
\regfield{(reserved)}{3}{9}{000}%
\regfield{H264\_DMA\_OUT\_MEM\_BURST\_LENGTH\_CH3}{3}{6}{{0x0}}%
\regfield{(reserved)}{1}{5}{0}%
\regfield{H264\_DMA\_OUT\_CHECK\_OWNER\_CH3}{1}{4}{{0}}%
\regfield{H264\_DMA\_OUT\_ECC\_AES\_EN\_CH3}{1}{3}{{0}}%
\regfield{H264\_DMA\_OUTDSCR\_BURST\_EN\_CH3}{1}{2}{{0}}%
\regfield{H264\_DMA\_OUT\_EOF\_MODE\_CH3}{1}{1}{{1}}%
\regfield{H264\_DMA\_OUT\_AUTO\_WRBACK\_CH3}{1}{0}{{0}}%
\reglabel{Reset}\regnewline%
\begin{regdesc}\begin{reglist}
\label{fielddesc:H264DMAOUTAUTOWRBACKCH3}\item [H264\_DMA\_OUT\_AUTO\_WRBACK\_CH3] Configures whether to enable automatic outlink-writeback when all the data pointed by outlink descriptor has been received.
\\0: Disable
\\1: Enable\\(R/W)
\label{fielddesc:H264DMAOUTEOFMODECH3}\item [H264\_DMA\_OUT\_EOF\_MODE\_CH3] Configures EOF flag generation mode for TX channel 3.
\\0: EOF flag is generated when last data has been pushed into FIFO in DMA
\\1: EOF flag is generated when last data has been popped from FIFO in DMA \\(R/W)
\label{fielddesc:H264DMAOUTDSCRBURSTENCH3}\item [H264\_DMA\_OUTDSCR\_BURST\_EN\_CH3] Configures whether to enable INCR burst transfer for TX channel 3 to read descriptors.\\
0: Disable\\
1: Enable\\(R/W)
\label{fielddesc:H264DMAOUTECCAESENCH3}\item [H264\_DMA\_OUT\_ECC\_AES\_EN\_CH3] Configures whether DMA can access external memory space for ECC and AES via TX channel 3.
\\0: Not access
\\1: Access ECC/AES area.In this case, the start address of the memory region should be 16-byte aligned. The product of the width and the bytes per pixel must also be 16-byte aligned.\\ (R/W)
\label{fielddesc:H264DMAOUTCHECKOWNERCH3}\item [H264\_DMA\_OUT\_CHECK\_OWNER\_CH3] Configures whether to enable owner bit check for TX channel 3.\\
0: Disable\\
1: Enable \\(R/W)

\item [Continued on the next page...]
\end{reglist}\end{regdesc}
\end{register}

\\1: AXI read data doesn't cross the address boundary\\(R/W)
\label{fielddesc:H264DMAINRSTCH0}\item [H264\_DMA\_IN\_RST\_CH0] Write 1 then write 0 to reset RX channel 0. (R/W)

\label{fielddesc:H264DMAINARBTOKENNUMCH0}\item [H264\_DMA\_IN\_ARB\_TOKEN\_NUM\_CH0] Configures the maximum token count for the arbiter configuration. (R/W)
\label{fielddesc:H264DMAEXTERINARBPRIORITYCH0}\item [H264\_DMA\_EXTER\_IN\_ARB\_PRIORITY\_CH0] Configures the priority of external memory access for RX channel 0. (R/W)
\label{fielddesc:H264DMAINTERINARBPRIORITYCH0}\item [H264\_DMA\_INTER\_IN\_ARB\_PRIORITY\_CH0] Configures the priority of internal memory access for RX channel 0. (R/W)
\end{reglist}\end{regdesc}
\end{register}

\begin{register}{H}{H264\_DMA\_IN\_RO\_PD\_CONF\_CH0\_REG}{0x0548}\label{regdesc:H264DMAINROPDCONFCH0REG}
\regfield{(reserved)}{25}{7}{0000000000000000000000000}%
\regfield{H264\_DMA\_IN\_RO\_RAM\_CLK\_FO\_CH0}{1}{6}{{0}}%
\regfield{(reserved)}{6}{0}{000000}%
\reglabel{Reset}\regnewline%
\begin{regdesc}\begin{reglist}
\label{fielddesc:H264DMAINRORAMCLKFOCH0}\item [H264\_DMA\_IN\_RO\_RAM\_CLK\_FO\_CH0] Configures whether to force enable clock gating for DMA RX reorder RAM.
\\0: A clock gating will be used when accessing the RAM in DMA
\\1: Force to open the clock and bypass the clock gating when accessing the RAM in DMA\\(R/W)
\end{reglist}\end{regdesc}
\end{register}


\begin{register}{H}{H264\_DMA\_IN\_CONF0\_CH1\_REG}{0x0600}\label{regdesc:H264DMAINCONF0CH1REG}
\regfield{(reserved)}{5}{27}{00000}%
\regfield{H264\_DMA\_IN\_ARB\_WEIGHT\_OPT\_DIS\_CH1}{1}{26}{{0}}%
\regfield{H264\_DMA\_IN\_CMD\_DISABLE\_CH1}{1}{25}{{0}}%
\regfield{H264\_DMA\_IN\_RST\_CH1}{1}{24}{{0}}%
\regfield{(reserved)}{11}{13}{00000000000}%
\regfield{H264\_DMA\_IN\_PAGE\_BOUND\_EN\_CH1}{1}{12}{{0}}%
\regfield{(reserved)}{3}{9}{000}%
\regfield{H264\_DMA\_IN\_MEM\_BURST\_LENGTH\_CH1}{3}{6}{{0x0}}%
\regfield{(reserved)}{1}{5}{0}%
\regfield{H264\_DMA\_IN\_CHECK\_OWNER\_CH1}{1}{4}{{0}}%
\regfield{H264\_DMA\_IN\_ECC\_AES\_EN\_CH1}{1}{3}{{0}}%
\regfield{H264\_DMA\_INDSCR\_BURST\_EN\_CH1}{1}{2}{{0}}%
\regfield{(reserved)}{2}{0}{00}%
\reglabel{Reset}\regnewline%
\begin{regdesc}\begin{reglist}
\label{fielddesc:H264DMAINDSCRBURSTENCH1}\item [H264\_DMA\_INDSCR\_BURST\_EN\_CH1] Configures whether to enable INCR burst transfer for RX channel 1 to read descriptors.\\
0: Disable\\
1: Enable\\(R/W)
\label{fielddesc:H264DMAINECCAESENCH1}\item [H264\_DMA\_IN\_ECC\_AES\_EN\_CH1] Configures whether DMA can access external memory space for ECC and AES via RX channel 1.\\
0: Not access\\
1: Access. In this case, the start address of the memory region should be 16-byte aligned. The product of the width and the bytes per pixel must also be 16-byte aligned.\\ (R/W)
\label{fielddesc:H264DMAINCHECKOWNERCH1}\item [H264\_DMA\_IN\_CHECK\_OWNER\_CH1] Configures whether to enable owner bit check for RX channel 1.\\
0: Disable\\
1: Enable \\(R/W)
\label{fielddesc:H264DMAINMEMBURSTLENGTHCH1}\item [H264\_DMA\_IN\_MEM\_BURST\_LENGTH\_CH1] Configures the burst length for RX channel 1.\\
0: 8 bytes\\
1: 16 bytes\\
2: 32 bytes\\
3: 64 bytes\\
4: 128 bytes\\
5 \verb+~+ 7: Invalid \\(R/W)
\label{fielddesc:H264DMAINPAGEBOUNDENCH1}\item [H264\_DMA\_IN\_PAGE\_BOUND\_EN\_CH1] Configures whether to make sure AXI read data doesn't cross the address boundary which define by mem\_burst\_length.
\\0: AXI read data can cross the address boundary
\\1: AXI read data doesn't cross the address boundary\\(R/W)
\label{fielddesc:H264DMAINRSTCH1}\item [H264\_DMA\_IN\_RST\_CH1] Write 1 then write 0 to reset RX channel 1. (R/W)

\item [Continued on the next page...]
\end{reglist}\end{regdesc}
\end{register}

1: Enable\\(R/W)
\label{fielddesc:H264DMAINARBWEIGHTOPTDISCH1}\item [H264\_DMA\_IN\_ARB\_WEIGHT\_OPT\_DIS\_CH1] Configures whether to disable weight arbitration for RX channel 1.\\
0: Enable\\
1: Disable \\(R/W)
\end{reglist}\end{regdesc}

\begin{register}{H}{H264\_DMA\_IN\_LINK\_CONF\_CH1\_REG}{0x061C}\label{regdesc:H264DMAINLINKCONFCH1REG}
\regfield{(reserved)}{7}{25}{0000000}%
\regfield{H264\_DMA\_INLINK\_PARK\_CH1}{1}{24}{{1}}%
\regfield{H264\_DMA\_INLINK\_RESTART\_CH1}{1}{23}{{0}}%
\regfield{H264\_DMA\_INLINK\_START\_CH1}{1}{22}{{0}}%
\regfield{H264\_DMA\_INLINK\_STOP\_CH1}{1}{21}{{0}}%
\regfield{H264\_DMA\_INLINK\_AUTO\_RET\_CH1}{1}{20}{{1}}%
\regfield{(reserved)}{20}{0}{00000000000000000000}%
\reglabel{Reset}\regnewline%
\begin{regdesc}\begin{reglist}
\label{fielddesc:H264DMAINLINKAUTORETCH1}\item [H264\_DMA\_INLINK\_AUTO\_RET\_CH1] Configures whether to return to the address of the current receive descriptor when there are errors during data reception.\\
0: Not return\\
1: Return\\(R/W)
\label{fielddesc:H264DMAINLINKSTOPCH1}\item [H264\_DMA\_INLINK\_STOP\_CH1] Configures whether to stop processing the inlink descriptors.\\
0: No effect\\
1: Stop\\ (R/W/SC)
\label{fielddesc:H264DMAINLINKSTARTCH1}\item [H264\_DMA\_INLINK\_START\_CH1] Configures whether to start processing the inlink descriptors.\\
0: No effect\\
1: Start \\(R/W/SC)
\label{fielddesc:H264DMAINLINKRESTARTCH1}\item [H264\_DMA\_INLINK\_RESTART\_CH1] Configures whether to restart a new inlink from the last address.\\
0: No effect\\
1: Restart\\(R/W/SC)
\label{fielddesc:H264DMAINLINKPARKCH1}\item [H264\_DMA\_INLINK\_PARK\_CH1] Represents the status of the inlink descriptor's FSM.
\\0: The inlink descriptor's FSM is working
\\1: The inlink descriptor's FSM is in idle state \\(RO)
\end{reglist}\end{regdesc}
\end{register}

\begin{register}{H}{H264\_DMA\_IN\_CONF0\_CH4\_REG}{0x0900}\label{regdesc:H264DMAINCONF0CH4REG}
\regfield{(reserved)}{5}{27}{00000}%
\regfield{H264\_DMA\_IN\_ARB\_WEIGHT\_OPT\_DIS\_CH4}{1}{26}{{0}}%
\regfield{H264\_DMA\_IN\_CMD\_DISABLE\_CH4}{1}{25}{{0}}%
\regfield{H264\_DMA\_IN\_RST\_CH4}{1}{24}{{0}}%
\regfield{(reserved)}{11}{13}{00000000000}%
\regfield{H264\_DMA\_IN\_PAGE\_BOUND\_EN\_CH4}{1}{12}{{0}}%
\regfield{(reserved)}{3}{9}{000}%
\regfield{H264\_DMA\_IN\_MEM\_BURST\_LENGTH\_CH4}{3}{6}{{0x0}}%
\regfield{(reserved)}{1}{5}{0}%
\regfield{H264\_DMA\_IN\_CHECK\_OWNER\_CH4}{1}{4}{{0}}%
\regfield{H264\_DMA\_IN\_ECC\_AES\_EN\_CH4}{1}{3}{{0}}%
\regfield{H264\_DMA\_INDSCR\_BURST\_EN\_CH4}{1}{2}{{0}}%
\regfield{(reserved)}{2}{0}{00}%
\reglabel{Reset}\regnewline%
\begin{regdesc}\begin{reglist}
\label{fielddesc:H264DMAINDSCRBURSTENCH4}\item [H264\_DMA\_INDSCR\_BURST\_EN\_CH4] Configures whether to enable INCR burst transfer for RX channel 4 to read descriptors.\\
0: Disable\\
1: Enable\\(R/W)
\label{fielddesc:H264DMAINECCAESENCH4}\item [H264\_DMA\_IN\_ECC\_AES\_EN\_CH4] Configures whether DMA can access external memory space for ECC and AES via RX channel 4.\\
0: Not access\\
1: Access. In this case, the start address of the memory region should be 16-byte aligned. The product of the width and the bytes per pixel must also be 16-byte aligned.\\ (R/W)
\label{fielddesc:H264DMAINCHECKOWNERCH4}\item [H264\_DMA\_IN\_CHECK\_OWNER\_CH4] Configures whether to enable owner bit check for RX channel 4.\\
0: Disable\\
1: Enable \\(R/W)
\label{fielddesc:H264DMAINMEMBURSTLENGTHCH4}\item [H264\_DMA\_IN\_MEM\_BURST\_LENGTH\_CH4] Configures the burst length for RX channel 4.\\
0: 8 bytes\\
1: 16 bytes\\
2: 32 bytes\\
3: 64 bytes\\
4: 128 bytes\\
5 \verb+~+ 7: Invalid \\(R/W)
\label{fielddesc:H264DMAINPAGEBOUNDENCH4}\item [H264\_DMA\_IN\_PAGE\_BOUND\_EN\_CH4] Configures whether to make sure AXI read data doesn't cross the address boundary which define by mem\_burst\_length.
\\0: AXI read data can cross the address boundary
\\1: AXI read data doesn't cross the address boundary\\(R/W)
\label{fielddesc:H264DMAINRSTCH4}\item [H264\_DMA\_IN\_RST\_CH4] Write 1 then write 0 to reset RX channel 4. (R/W)

\item [Continued on the next page...]
\end{reglist}\end{regdesc}
\end{register}


\addtocounter{Regfloat}{-1}
\begin{register}{H}{H264\_DMA\_IN\_CONF0\_CH4\_REG}{0x0900}
\begin{regdesc}\begin{reglist}
\item [Continued from the previous page...]

\label{fielddesc:H264DMAINCMDDISABLECH4}\item [H264\_DMA\_IN\_CMD\_DISABLE\_CH4] Configures whether to disable command on RX channel 4.\\
0: Disable\\
1: Enable\\(R/W)
\label{fielddesc:H264DMAINARBWEIGHTOPTDISCH4}\item [H264\_DMA\_IN\_ARB\_WEIGHT\_OPT\_DIS\_CH4] Configures whether to disable weight arbitration for RX channel 4.\\
0: Enable\\
1: Disable \\(R/W)
\end{reglist}\end{regdesc}
\end{register}


\begin{register}{H}{H264\_DMA\_IN\_POP\_CH4\_REG}{0x0918}\label{regdesc:H264DMAINPOPCH4REG}
\regfield{(reserved)}{20}{12}{00000000000000000000}%
\regfield{H264\_DMA\_INFIFO\_POP\_CH4}{1}{11}{{0}}%
\regfield{H264\_DMA\_INFIFO\_RDATA\_CH4}{11}{0}{{0x400}}%
\reglabel{Reset}\regnewline%
\begin{regdesc}\begin{reglist}
\label{fielddesc:H264DMAINFIFORDATACH4}\item [H264\_DMA\_INFIFO\_RDATA\_CH4] Represents the data popped from DMA RX FIFO. (RO)
\label{fielddesc:H264DMAINFIFOPOPCH4}\item [H264\_DMA\_INFIFO\_POP\_CH4] Configures whether to pop data from DMA RX FIFO.\\
0: No effect\\
1: Pop\\ (R/W/SC)
\end{reglist}\end{regdesc}
\end{register}


\begin{register}{H}{H264\_DMA\_IN\_LINK\_CONF\_CH4\_REG}{0x091C}\label{regdesc:H264DMAINLINKCONFCH4REG}
\regfield{(reserved)}{7}{25}{0000000}%
\regfield{H264\_DMA\_INLINK\_PARK\_CH4}{1}{24}{{1}}%
\regfield{H264\_DMA\_INLINK\_RESTART\_CH4}{1}{23}{{0}}%
\regfield{H264\_DMA\_INLINK\_START\_CH4}{1}{22}{{0}}%
\regfield{H264\_DMA\_INLINK\_STOP\_CH4}{1}{21}{{0}}%
\regfield{H264\_DMA\_INLINK\_AUTO\_RET\_CH4}{1}{20}{{1}}%
\regfield{(reserved)}{20}{0}{00000000000000000000}%
\reglabel{Reset}\regnewline%
\begin{regdesc}\begin{reglist}
\label{fielddesc:H264DMAINLINKAUTORETCH4}\item [H264\_DMA\_INLINK\_AUTO\_RET\_CH4] Configures whether to return to the address of the current receive descriptor when there are errors during data reception.\\
0: Not return\\
1: Return\\(R/W)
\label{fielddesc:H264DMAINLINKSTOPCH4}\item [H264\_DMA\_INLINK\_STOP\_CH4] Configures whether to stop processing the inlink descriptors.\\
0: No effect\\
1: Stop\\ (R/W/SC)
\label{fielddesc:H264DMAINLINKSTARTCH4}\item [H264\_DMA\_INLINK\_START\_CH4] Configures whether to start processing the inlink descriptors.\\
0: No effect\\
1: Start \\(R/W/SC)
\label{fielddesc:H264DMAINLINKRESTARTCH4}\item [H264\_DMA\_INLINK\_RESTART\_CH4] Configures whether to restart a new inlink from the last address.\\
0: No effect\\
1: Restart\\(R/W/SC)
\label{fielddesc:H264DMAINLINKPARKCH4}\item [H264\_DMA\_INLINK\_PARK\_CH4] Represents the status of the inlink descriptor's FSM.
\\0: The inlink descriptor's FSM is working
\\1: The inlink descriptor's FSM is in idle state \\(RO)
\end{reglist}\end{regdesc}
\end{register}

\begin{register}{H}{H264\_DMA\_IN\_LINK\_ADDR\_CH4\_REG}{0x0920}\label{regdesc:H264DMAINLINKADDRCH4REG}
\regfield{H264\_DMA\_INLINK\_ADDR\_CH4}{32}{0}{{0x000000}}%
\reglabel{Reset}\regnewline%
\begin{regdesc}\begin{reglist}
\label{fielddesc:H264DMAINLINKADDRCH4}\item [H264\_DMA\_INLINK\_ADDR\_CH4] Configures the first inlink descriptor's address. (R/W)
\end{reglist}\end{regdesc}
\end{register}

\begin{register}{H}{H264\_DMA\_IN\_CONF0\_CH5\_REG}{0x0A00}\label{regdesc:H264DMAINCONF0CH5REG}

0: Not access\\
1: Access. In this case, the start address of the memory region should be 16-byte aligned. The product of the width and the bytes per pixel must also be 16-byte aligned.\\ (R/W)
\label{fielddesc:H264DMAINMEMBURSTLENGTHCH5}\item [H264\_DMA\_IN\_MEM\_BURST\_LENGTH\_CH5] Configures the burst length for RX channel 5.\\
0: 8 bytes\\
1: 16 bytes\\
2: 32 bytes\\
3: 64 bytes\\
4: 128 bytes\\
5 \verb+~+ 7: Invalid \\(R/W)
\label{fielddesc:H264DMAINPAGEBOUNDENCH5}\item [H264\_DMA\_IN\_PAGE\_BOUND\_EN\_CH5] Configures whether to make sure AXI read data doesn't cross the address boundary which define by mem\_burst\_length.
\\0: AXI read data can cross the address boundary
\\1: AXI read data doesn't cross the address boundary\\(R/W)
\label{fielddesc:H264DMAINRSTCH5}\item [H264\_DMA\_IN\_RST\_CH5] Write 1 then write 0 to reset RX channel 5. (R/W)
\label{fielddesc:H264DMAINCMDDISABLECH5}\item [H264\_DMA\_IN\_CMD\_DISABLE\_CH5] Configures whether to disable command on RX channel 5.\\
0: Disable\\
1: Enable\\(R/W)
\end{reglist}\end{regdesc}
\end{register}

\begin{register}{H}{H264\_DMA\_RST\_CONF\_REG}{0x0B08}\label{regdesc:H264DMARSTCONFREG}

\label{fielddesc:H264DMAINTERAXIMWRRST}\item [H264\_DMA\_INTER\_AXIM\_WR\_RST] Write 1 and then 0 to reset the inter AXI write FSM. (R/W)
\label{fielddesc:H264DMAEXTERAXIMRDRST}\item [H264\_DMA\_EXTER\_AXIM\_RD\_RST] Write 1 and then 0 to reset the exter AXI read FSM. (R/W)
\label{fielddesc:H264DMAEXTERAXIMWRRST}\item [H264\_DMA\_EXTER\_AXIM\_WR\_RST] Write 1 and then 0 to reset the exter AXI write FSM. (R/W)
\label{fielddesc:H264DMACLKEN}\item [H264\_DMA\_CLK\_EN] Configures DMA clock gating.\\

1: Always enable the clock for registers \\(R/W)
\end{reglist}\end{regdesc}
\end{register}

\begin{register}{H}{H264\_DMA\_OUT\_INT\_RAW\_CH0\_REG}{0x0004}\label{regdesc:H264DMAOUTINTRAWCH0REG}
\regfield{(reserved)}{23}{9}{00000000000000000000000}%
\regfield{H264\_DMA\_OUT\_DSCR\_TASK\_OVF\_CH0\_INT\_RAW}{1}{8}{{0}}%

\regfield{H264\_DMA\_OUTFIFO\_OVF\_L2\_CH0\_INT\_RAW}{1}{6}{{0}}%

\regfield{H264\_DMA\_OUTFIFO\_OVF\_L1\_CH0\_INT\_RAW}{1}{4}{{0}}%

\begin{regdesc}\begin{reglist}

\regfield{H264\_DMA\_OUTFIFO\_CNT\_L1\_CH0}{5}{8}{{0x0}}%

1: Full \\(RO)
\label{fielddesc:H264DMAOUTFIFOEMPTYL2CH0}\item [H264\_DMA\_OUTFIFO\_EMPTY\_L2\_CH0] Represents whether l2 FIFO of TX channel 0 is empty.\\
0: Not empty\\
1: Empty\\ (RO)
\label{fielddesc:H264DMAOUTFIFOCNTL2CH0}\item [H264\_DMA\_OUTFIFO\_CNT\_L2\_CH0] Represents the data quantity in l2 FIFO for TX channel 0. Measurement unit: 16 bytes. (RO)
\label{fielddesc:H264DMAOUTFIFOFULLL1CH0}\item [H264\_DMA\_OUTFIFO\_FULL\_L1\_CH0] Represents whether l1 FIFO of TX channel 0 is full.\\
0: Not Full\\
1: Full \\(RO)
\label{fielddesc:H264DMAOUTFIFOEMPTYL1CH0}\item [H264\_DMA\_OUTFIFO\_EMPTY\_L1\_CH0] Represents whether l1 FIFO of TX channel 0 is empty.\\
0: Not empty\\
1: Empty\\ (RO)
\label{fielddesc:H264DMAOUTFIFOCNTL1CH0}\item [H264\_DMA\_OUTFIFO\_CNT\_L1\_CH0] Represents the data quantity in l1 FIFO for TX channel 0. Measurement unit: byte. (RO)
\label{fielddesc:H264DMAOUTFIFOFULLL3CH0}\item [H264\_DMA\_OUTFIFO\_FULL\_L3\_CH0] Represents whether l3 FIFO of TX channel 0 is full.\\
0: Not Full\\
1: Full \\(RO)
\label{fielddesc:H264DMAOUTFIFOEMPTYL3CH0}\item [H264\_DMA\_OUTFIFO\_EMPTY\_L3\_CH0] Represents whether l3 FIFO of TX channel 0 is empty.\\
0: Not empty\\
1: Empty\\ (RO)
\label{fielddesc:H264DMAOUTFIFOCNTL3CH0}\item [H264\_DMA\_OUTFIFO\_CNT\_L3\_CH0] Represents the data quantity in l3 FIFO for TX channel 0. Measurement unit: 8 bytes. (RO)
\end{reglist}\end{regdesc}
\end{register}

\label{fielddesc:H264DMAOUTRESETAVAILCH0}\item [H264\_DMA\_OUT\_RESET\_AVAIL\_CH0] Represents whether it is safe to reset the channel.
\\0: Unsafe
\\1: Safe \\(RO)

\regfield{H264\_DMA\_OUTFIFO\_CNT\_L3\_CH3}{2}{18}{{0x0}}%
\regfield{H264\_DMA\_OUTFIFO\_EMPTY\_L3\_CH3}{1}{17}{{1}}%
\regfield{H264\_DMA\_OUTFIFO\_FULL\_L3\_CH3}{1}{16}{{0}}%
\regfield{(reserved)}{3}{13}{000}%
\regfield{H264\_DMA\_OUTFIFO\_CNT\_L1\_CH3}{5}{8}{{0x0}}%
\regfield{H264\_DMA\_OUTFIFO\_EMPTY\_L1\_CH3}{1}{7}{{1}}%
\regfield{H264\_DMA\_OUTFIFO\_FULL\_L1\_CH3}{1}{6}{{0}}%
\regfield{H264\_DMA\_OUTFIFO\_CNT\_L2\_CH3}{4}{2}{{0x0}}%
\regfield{H264\_DMA\_OUTFIFO\_EMPTY\_L2\_CH3}{1}{1}{{1}}%
\regfield{H264\_DMA\_OUTFIFO\_FULL\_L2\_CH3}{1}{0}{{0}}%
\reglabel{Reset}\regnewline%
\begin{regdesc}\begin{reglist}
\label{fielddesc:H264DMAOUTFIFOFULLL2CH3}\item [H264\_DMA\_OUTFIFO\_FULL\_L2\_CH3] Represents whether l2 FIFO of TX channel 3 is full.\\
0: Not Full\\
1: Full \\(RO)
\label{fielddesc:H264DMAOUTFIFOEMPTYL2CH3}\item [H264\_DMA\_OUTFIFO\_EMPTY\_L2\_CH3] Represents whether l2 FIFO of TX channel 3 is empty.\\
0: Not empty\\
1: Empty\\ (RO)
\label{fielddesc:H264DMAOUTFIFOCNTL2CH3}\item [H264\_DMA\_OUTFIFO\_CNT\_L2\_CH3] Represents the data quantity in l2 FIFO for TX channel 3. Measurement unit: 16 bytes. (RO)
\label{fielddesc:H264DMAOUTFIFOFULLL1CH3}\item [H264\_DMA\_OUTFIFO\_FULL\_L1\_CH3] Represents whether l1 FIFO of TX channel 3 is full.\\
0: Not Full\\
1: Full \\(RO)
\label{fielddesc:H264DMAOUTFIFOEMPTYL1CH3}\item [H264\_DMA\_OUTFIFO\_EMPTY\_L1\_CH3] Represents whether l1 FIFO of TX channel 3 is empty.\\
0: Not empty\\
1: Empty\\ (RO)
\label{fielddesc:H264DMAOUTFIFOCNTL1CH3}\item [H264\_DMA\_OUTFIFO\_CNT\_L1\_CH3] Represents the data quantity in l1 FIFO for TX channel 3. Measurement unit: byte. (RO)
\label{fielddesc:H264DMAOUTFIFOFULLL3CH3}\item [H264\_DMA\_OUTFIFO\_FULL\_L3\_CH3] Represents whether l3 FIFO of TX channel 3 is full.\\
0: Not Full\\
1: Full \\(RO)
\label{fielddesc:H264DMAOUTFIFOEMPTYL3CH3}\item [H264\_DMA\_OUTFIFO\_EMPTY\_L3\_CH3] Represents whether l3 FIFO of TX channel 3 is empty.\\
0: Not empty\\
1: Empty\\ (RO)
\label{fielddesc:H264DMAOUTFIFOCNTL3CH3}\item [H264\_DMA\_OUTFIFO\_CNT\_L3\_CH3] Represents the data quantity in l3 FIFO for TX channel 3. Measurement unit: 8 bytes. (RO)
\end{reglist}\end{regdesc}
\end{register}

\regfield{H264\_DMA\_EXTER\_RD\_BAK\_FIFO\_CNT}{4}{15}{{0x0}}%
\regfield{H264\_DMA\_EXTER\_RD\_FIFO\_CNT}{3}{12}{{0x0}}%
\regfield{H264\_DMA\_EXTER\_WRESP\_ERR\_CNT}{4}{8}{{0x0}}%
\regfield{H264\_DMA\_EXTER\_RRESP\_ERR\_CNT}{4}{4}{{0x0}}%
\regfield{H264\_DMA\_EXTER\_RID\_ERR\_CNT}{4}{0}{{0x0}}%
\reglabel{Reset}\regnewline%
\begin{regdesc}\begin{reglist}
\label{fielddesc:H264DMAEXTERRIDERRCNT}\item [H264\_DMA\_EXTER\_RID\_ERR\_CNT] Represents the count of errors in the external memory ID for AXI read. (RO)
\label{fielddesc:H264DMAEXTERRRESPERRCNT}\item [H264\_DMA\_EXTER\_RRESP\_ERR\_CNT] Represents the count of errors in the response for external memory during AXI read operations. (RO)
\label{fielddesc:H264DMAEXTERWRESPERRCNT}\item [H264\_DMA\_EXTER\_WRESP\_ERR\_CNT] Represents the count of AXI write external memory resp err. (RO)
\label{fielddesc:H264DMAEXTERRDFIFOCNT}\item [H264\_DMA\_EXTER\_RD\_FIFO\_CNT] Represents the count of cmd FIFO remain cmd in AXI read external memory module.  (RO)
\label{fielddesc:H264DMAEXTERRDBAKFIFOCNT}\item [H264\_DMA\_EXTER\_RD\_BAK\_FIFO\_CNT] Represents the count of backup cmd FIFO remain cmd in AXI read external memory module.(RO)
\label{fielddesc:H264DMAEXTERWRFIFOCNT}\item [H264\_DMA\_EXTER\_WR\_FIFO\_CNT] Represents the count of cmd FIFO remain cmd in AXI write external memory module. (RO)
\label{fielddesc:H264DMAEXTERWRBAKFIFOCNT}\item [H264\_DMA\_EXTER\_WR\_BAK\_FIFO\_CNT] Represents the count of backup cmd FIFO remain cmd in AXI write external memory module. (RO)
\end{reglist}\end{regdesc}
\end{register}
